msg:‚ù§Reason for recommendation:
The Beiluo Secret Realm Resort on Hailing Island, Yangjiang has become the first local Internet celebrity in the past two years. There are two apar**ent-type hotels here, Beiluo Secretland Resort Hotel and Beiluo Secretland Luoyue Hotel, as well as four major swimming pools, private beaches, mountain parks and other good places for vacation and play, and all kinds of photos are stunning. Beiluo has no obvious shortcomings except for being expensive.

üóìItinerary:
It is best to set aside a whole day for Beiluo Secret Realm Resort, because there are many places to play besides accommodation. There are four must-check spots here.
‚úÖMust experience 1: Private beach. Beiluo Resort and Beiluo Secret Realm share a private beach in Beiluo Bay. There are relatively few tourists here, the sand is cleaner, and there are many internet celebrity props for taking pictures.
‚úÖMust experience 2: Skyline Pool. On the top floor of the 30th floor of the resort, it is open to resort guests only at no additional charge.
‚úÖMust experience 3: Mountain Park. Mountain Park is open to guests of both hotels, and most room rate packages already include tickets. The park was originally a wild mountain, but this is the only way to get to the cliff pool. There is not much scenery on the way out, and the return trip can overlook the entire Beiluo Bay is very spectacular. A trip back and forth does not count for 40 minutes of taking pictures.
‚úÖMust experience 4: Cliff Pool. There is a separate fee for the cliff pool, which is not included in most hotel packages. Sightseeing tickets are 50/adult, half price for children over 1 meter. Swimming tickets are 298/person. Although you can see some swimming pools from the mountain park, it is very different from the experience of playing in the water by the swimming pool. This sightseeing ticket is not recommended.

üè®Hotel environment: The interior decoration of the resort hotel is average, partial to the apar**ent grade, all room types can look out to the sea, unfortunately all the windows are closed [Facepalm]
üñºRestaurant environment: There are several restaurants in Beiluo. Including the resort's western restaurant/breakfast restaurant, Shunfeng Chinese restaurant, and outsourced barbecue stalls on the beach at night. Didn't go to the restaurant, went to the BBQ stall. Although the a**osphere here is very good, it is expensive, 5 strings per person plus a bottle of Corona is 75.
